Thought for 10s Yes — now you’re thinking like a founder. You do not need to “redo Spotify.” For the MVP you described, you only need a clean fan app / label hub with three core things: Artist/music pages User accounts / profiles Email signup + subscriber list That is very doable. What you already have: a computer storage your music/catalog your brand What you still need is mostly the software stack and a few business basics. What the MVP should include For your first version, I’d keep it to: Home page for Ultra Music Group Artist pages Release pages Links or embedded playback to Spotify / Apple / YouTube Fan signup User login Simple user profiles A “favorites” or “follow artists” feature Admin area for you to update artists and releases That’s enough to feel real without getting too heavy. What you need to build it You’ll want these pieces: 1. Front end This is the actual app people see. A common modern route is Expo / React Native, which lets you build for Android, iOS, and web from one JavaScript/TypeScript project. Expo’s docs describe it as a way to build one project that runs natively across devices. 2. Database + accounts You need somewhere to store: users profiles artists releases favorites email subscribers Two strong options are Supabase or Firebase. Supabase gives you a Postgres database, authentication, storage, APIs, and realtime features in one platform. Firebase also gives you authentication and a scalable database. Firebase Auth supports email/password sign-in and password reset flows, and Firestore is designed for mobile and web apps with realtime syncing. 3. Email system For your subscriber list, you need an email service to collect signups and send updates. Resend provides email sending APIs plus audience/broadcast tools, and they also note that new domains should be warmed up gradually for deliverability. 4. Storage Even if you are not hosting full songs yourself yet, you’ll still want storage for: artist photos cover art banners profile images Supabase and Firebase both support storage alongside auth/database. 5. App deployment If you want an actual phone app later, Expo’s EAS Build is the piece that turns the project into store-ready app builds. What you probably do not need yet You do not need: your own music streaming engine your own audio CDN subscriptions with paid billing on day one complicated AI features a giant server setup For version 1, let Spotify/Apple/YouTube handle playback and let your app be the home base. Best setup for you For your specific idea, I’d recommend this stack: Expo for the app Supabase for users, profiles, database, storage Resend for email signups and announcements Why this combo: It covers app + login + profiles + email It’s lighter than building a giant custom backend from scratch It gives you room to grow later Extra things you need besides tech This part matters too: Domain name for Ultra Music Group Brand email like hello@ or support@ Privacy Policy Terms of Service app store accounts later, if you want mobile release a clear content plan for what users do after signing up Because once people create profiles, you need to answer: “Why should they come back?” Good MVP answers: save favorite artists get early release alerts receive exclusive updates join the subscriber list unlock special announcements Smart features to add first The “cool” thing you were asking about is not just profiles. It’s giving profiles a purpose. I’d add: follow favorite artist save favorite releases email me when new music drops birthday field for fan rewards later city/country field so you learn where fans are simple profile photo + username That makes your app feel like a real fan club platform, not just a website. What you need from a practical standpoint To actually start, you need: laptop/computer internet app name logo / cover assets artist bios and photos release list domain one backend choice one email provider one clear MVP feature list That’s it. Founder-level advice Your first MVP should answer only one question: “Why would a fan sign up today?” A strong answer would be: “Create your Ultra profile, follow your favorite artists, and get first access to new releases, visuals, and special drops.” That’s enough. My honest recommendation Don’t start with a giant app brief. Start with this exact MVP: splash screen home page artist list artist profile pages release pages account creation user profile favorites/follow email signup admin dashboard for you That is the right first build. Keep going 👇 Updated Thought for 18s Perfect. Now the next smart move is to preview it in a browser so you can actually see the app. Go to Settings in that repo, then in the left sidebar click Pages. Under Build and deployment, set Source to Deploy from a branch, then choose the main branch and the root (/) folder, and save. GitHub’s Pages docs say that branch deployment is the simple route when you do not need a custom build process, and that index.html works as a valid entry file. After that, GitHub will publish a public Pages site for the repo. Public repositories can use GitHub Pages, and the site is publicly accessible once published. If you get a 404 at first, that usually just means Pages has not finished publishing yet, or there is an issue with the entry file or folder selection. GitHub’s troubleshooting guide specifically calls out 404s and checking that index.html is present in the published source. Good question — let me break it down super simple so you actually understand it (not just follow it). 🟡 First — the names (you mixed them a little) PNG ✅ (correct) JPG / JPEG ✅ (this is what you meant by “GPAG”) There is no “GPAG” — you meant JPG 🟢 PNG vs JPG (REAL difference) 🟡 PNG Better quality Keeps sharp details (like text, logos, glow) Supports transparency (no background) Bigger file size 🔵 JPG Compresses image (loses a little quality) Smaller file size No transparency Better for photos, not logos 🔥 WHY YOUR LOGO SHOULD BE PNG Your logo is: Gold Glowing Detailed Has sharp text (“ULTRA MUSIC GROUP”) 👉 JPG will slightly blur it 👉 PNG keeps it crisp and clean That’s why: 👉 Use PNG for logos 👉 Use JPG for artist photos 💡 EASY RULE (remember this forever) Type Use Logo PNG Artist pictures JPG Album covers JPG or PNG ⚠️ BUT HERE’S THE REAL TRUTH Your website doesn’t care. About Ultra Music Group

Ultra Music Group is an independent record label built to develop original artists, release new music, and create a unified world of sound, visuals, and identity. The label brings together a growing roster across pop, Latin, electronic, and crossover music with a focus on strong songwriting, memorable characters, and cinematic presentation.

Every release is part of a larger creative vision — from the music itself to the visuals, branding, artist development, and digital experience. Ultra Music Group is designed as a next-generation independent label built from the ground up with ambition, consistency, and long-term world-building at its core.

Independent label concept, music development, and creative direction by Juan Pablo Ochoa.

About Ultra Music Group

Ultra Music Group is an independent creative music label founded by Juan Pablo Ochoa and built from the ground up to develop original artists, release new music, and create a unified world of sound, visuals, and identity.

The label brings together a growing roster across pop, Latin, electronic, and crossover music, with a focus on strong songwriting, memorable characters, cinematic presentation, and long-term world-building.

Every release is part of a larger creative vision — from the music itself to the visuals, artist development, branding, and digital experience. Ultra Music Group is designed as a next-generation independent label built on creativity, consistency, innovation, and emotional storytelling.

Independent label concept, music development, and creative direction by Juan Pablo Ochoa.

Ultra Music Group © 2026
Paste this block:

Mission Statement

Ultra Music Group is an independent creative music label founded by Juan Pablo Ochoa, a songwriter, creator, and developer dedicated to building a new generation of musical storytelling through virtual artists and digital performers.

  • At Ultra Music Group, every artist begins as an idea — a character, a personality, and a world.
  • From concept to creation, Juan Pablo develops each project from the ground up: writing the music, shaping the identity of the artist, designing the visual universe, and building a catalog of songs that express emotion, movement, and imagination.
  • Transparency, creativity, and artistic experimentation are central to the label’s foundation.
  • Some Ultra Music Group productions use AI-assisted vocal technology and digital performance tools, and that process is shared openly with the audience. Technology is treated as a creative instrument — just like a synthesizer, microphone, or studio.

What defines Ultra Music Group is not the technology behind the music, but the heart behind the creation.

Every song, every artist, and every project released by Ultra Music Group is part of a larger vision — a creative universe where characters, music, and imagination come together to form something greater than any single song.

Founded by Juan Pablo Ochoa.

About Ultra Music Group

Ultra Music Group is an independent creative music label founded by Juan Pablo Ochoa and built from the ground up to develop original artists, release new music, and create a unified world of sound, visuals, and identity.

The label brings together a growing roster across pop, Latin, electronic, and crossover music, with a focus on strong songwriting, memorable characters, cinematic presentation, and long-term world-building.

Every release is part of a larger creative vision — from the music itself to the visuals, artist development, branding, and digital experience. Ultra Music Group is designed as a next-generation independent label built on creativity, consistency, innovation, and emotional storytelling.

Independent label concept, music development, and creative direction by Juan Pablo Ochoa.

Mission Statement

Ultra Music Group is an independent creative music label founded by Juan Pablo Ochoa, a songwriter, creator, and developer dedicated to building a new generation of musical storytelling through virtual artists and digital performers.

  • At Ultra Music Group, every artist begins as an idea — a character, a personality, and a world.
  • From concept to creation, Juan Pablo develops each project from the ground up: writing the music, shaping the identity of the artist, designing the visual universe, and building a catalog of songs that express emotion, movement, and imagination.
  • Transparency, creativity, and artistic experimentation are central to the label’s foundation.
  • Some Ultra Music Group productions use AI-assisted vocal technology and digital performance tools, and that process is shared openly with the audience. Technology is treated as a creative instrument — just like a synthesizer, microphone, or studio.

What defines Ultra Music Group is not the technology behind the music, but the heart behind the creation.

Every song, every artist, and every project released by Ultra Music Group is part of a larger vision — a creative universe where characters, music, and imagination come together to form something greater than any single song.

Founded by Juan Pablo Ochoa.

File 2: manifest.json Create a new file named manifest.json and paste this: { "name": "Ultra Music Group", "short_name": "Ultra Music", "description": "Official Ultra Music Group artist roster and releases", "start_url": "./", "scope": "./", "display": "standalone", "background_color": "#050505", "theme_color": "#000000", "icons": [ { "src": "logo.png", "sizes": "192x192", "type": "image/png" }, { "src": "logo.png", "sizes": "512x512", "type": "image/png" } ] } File 3: service-worker.js Create a new file named service-worker.js and paste this: const CACHE_NAME = 'ultra-music-group-v1'; const ASSETS_TO_CACHE = [ './', './index.html', './manifest.json', './logo.png' ]; self.addEventListener('install', event => { event.waitUntil( caches.open(CACHE_NAME).then(cache => cache.addAll(ASSETS_TO_CACHE)) ); self.skipWaiting(); }); self.addEventListener('activate', event => { event.waitUntil( caches.keys().then(keys => Promise.all( keys.map(key => { if (key !== CACHE_NAME) { return caches.delete(key); } }) ) ) ); self.clients.claim(); }); self.addEventListener('fetch', event => { event.respondWith( caches.match(event.request).then(cached => cached || fetch(event.request)) ); }); Then do this Upload all 3: index.html manifest.json service-worker.js Make sure logo.png is already in the repo. A Record — Host: @ → 185.199.108.153 A Record — Host: @ → 185.199.109.153 A Record — Host: @ → 185.199.110.153 A Record — Host: @ → 185.199.111.153 CNAME Record — Host: www → ultrafilmsholdings-boop.github.io 2. In your GitHub repo, set the custom domain to: ultramusicgroup.com GitHub says custom domains for branch-based Pages sites are stored in a CNAME file at the root of the publishing source, or you can set it in the repository’s Pages settings. So use either: Settings → Pages → Custom domain → enter ultramusicgroup.com or create a file named CNAME containing exactly: ultramusicgroup.com 3. Save everything and wait. DNS changes can take a bit to propagate, and GitHub says HTTPS may take up to about an hour after the custom domain is configured correctly. If you want, I can also show you one very powerful post idea that labels use after the launch that can make your page look even more like a major label. Yes — there is a very common “post-launch playbook” trick that record labels use after they introduce a roster. It’s simple, but it makes the label look much bigger and more established overnight. It’s called the “Meet the Artists / Universe Post.” After the mission statement and first releases, labels create a post that introduces the entire world of the label, not just the songs. 🔥 The Powerful Post Idea: “Meet the Artists of Ultra Music Group” The goal is to make it feel like a full musical universe, not just a few singles. You already almost did this with your roster image — but the caption can make it much stronger. Example Post Caption Meet the Artists of Ultra Music Group™ A new generation of music is here. Ultra Music Group was founded by songwriter and creator Juan Pablo Ochoa to build a universe of artists, sounds, and stories through creativity and imagination. Introducing the artists of Ultra Music Group: 🎤 Juan Pablo – Hearts on the Highway  🤠 Ángel Valentín – Corazón de Acero  🍒 Lily Hart – Cherry Soda  💙 Jax Monroe – Electric Blue Heart  ✨ Aria Nova – Hearts on the Highway  💍 Luca Valley – When We Say I Do  🌅 Neon Euphoria – Electric Afterglow  🌍 Niko Sol – Global Heartbeat  🌙 Elena Star – Ángel de Neón Each artist represents a different sound, energy, and atmosphere — from pop and dance to cinematic and electronic music. Together they form the creative universe of Ultra Music Group™. Building tomorrow’s hitmakers. Why labels do this post It accomplishes three things: 1️⃣ Legitimacy  It shows the label has a full roster. 2️⃣ Worldbuilding  Fans start to understand the identity of the label. 3️⃣ Discovery  People might come for one artist and discover others. One more powerful post labels use next After that roster post, labels often post something like: “Which artist are you listening to?” Example caption: The artists of Ultra Music Group are officially streaming worldwide. Discover the Ultra Music Group roster

Explore the official lineup, starting with flagship artist Juan Pablo, followed by the full roster, interactive player, artist bios, and current worldwide releases.

About Ultra Music Group™

Ultra Music Group is an independent creative music label founded by Juan Pablo Ochoa and built from the ground up to develop original artists, release new music, and create a unified world of sound, visuals, character, and identity through visual storytelling.

The label is designed as a full creative universe where every artist begins as an idea — a personality, a perspective, a sound, and a world. From concept to creation, Juan Pablo develops each project from the ground up: writing the music, shaping the artistic identity, designing the visual atmosphere, and building a catalog of songs that express emotion, movement, imagination, and cinematic energy.

Ultra Music Group spans multiple genres and creative lanes, including pop, cinematic pop, dance pop, crossover pop, Latin pop, reggaeton, Latin urban, Latin dance, electronic music, euphoric music, R&B, soul, blues, jazz, country, pop-country, regional Mexican, norteño, banda, banda norteña, ranchera, corridos, and genre-blending contemporary music built for both mainstream and character-driven storytelling.

What defines Ultra Music Group is not just the variety of its sound, but the intention behind the work. Every release is part of a larger creative vision — from the music itself to the visuals, artist development, branding, cinematic presentation, and digital experience. The goal is not simply to release songs, but to build an immersive label ecosystem where music and imagination come together in a way that feels alive.

Transparency, creativity, and artistic experimentation are core values of Ultra Music Group. Some productions use AI-assisted vocal technology and digital performance tools, and that process is openly shared with the audience. Technology is treated as a creative instrument — just like a synthesizer, microphone, camera, or studio — while the emotional core, writing, and vision remain at the center of every project.

Ultra Music Group is built for listeners who want more than a single track. It is a label universe designed around sound, atmosphere, character, movement, and emotional impact.

Music should inspire people to feel alive. Founded by Juan Pablo Ochoa.

ULTRA MUSIC GROUP™ — Mission Statement

Ultra Music Group is an independent creative music label founded by Juan Pablo Ochoa, a songwriter, creator, and developer dedicated to building a new generation of musical storytelling through virtual artists and digital performers.

At Ultra Music Group, every artist begins as an idea — a character, a personality, and a world.

From concept to creation, Juan Pablo develops each project from the ground up: writing the music, shaping the identity of the artist, designing the visual universe, and building a catalog of songs that express emotion, movement, and imagination.

Transparency, creativity, and artistic experimentation are core values of Ultra Music Group.

Some Ultra Music Group productions use AI-assisted vocal technology and digital performance tools, and we openly share that process with our audience. Technology is simply a creative instrument — just like a synthesizer, microphone, or studio.

What defines Ultra Music Group is not the technology behind the music, but the heart behind the creation.

Every song, every artist, and every project released by Ultra Music Group is part of a larger vision — a creative universe where characters, music, and imagination come together to form something greater than any single song.

At the center of that vision is one guiding belief:

Music should inspire people to feel alive.

Founded by Juan Pablo Ochoa

Ultra Music Group © 2026

ultramusicgroup@gmail.com

Private catalog available for labels, artists, and industry professionals upon request.
